 > [CLI AGENT PROMPT]
   CONTEXT (COLD START - READ CAREFULLY):
   You are jumping into an active C++ OpenGL project (`AliceViewer`). It features a 3-Tier FBO pipeline that extracts Beauty, Segmentation, and
   Depth maps, compresses them to PNGs via `stb_image` in a background thread, Base64 encodes them, and sends them to the Gemini Vision API using
   `cpp-httplib` (compiled with Windows SChannel/MbedTLS).
   The local memory architecture, FBO blitting, and TLS network layers are currently stable and compiling with 0 errors. However, the API request
   is returning an HTTP 404 because the hardcoded model endpoint is incorrect, and the API key needs updating. We also need explicit file-based
   logging to validate network success autonomously.

   EXECUTION MANDATE:
   Open `include/AliceGeminiClient.h`. Execute autonomously. Do not ask for permission. Complete success is defined as an HTTP 200 OK with a JSON
   text body.

   1. UPDATE API KEY & ENDPOINT:
      - In `workerThreadFunc`, locate the fallback hardcoded test key and update it exactly:
        `apiKey = "AIzaSyBPQ7zpS_YGZhA6CHE1bLWbwXxBVArGvbk";`
      - Update the `httplib::Client` POST path to use the correct multimodal model (`gemini-1.5-flash`). It MUST be this exact string:
        `auto res = cli.Post("/v1beta/models/gemini-1.5-flash:generateContent", json, "application/json");`

   2. EXPLICIT FILE LOGGING:
      - Ensure `<fstream>` is included at the top of the file.
      - In `workerThreadFunc`, locate the HTTP execution block (`auto res = cli.Post(...)`). Replace the subsequent `if (res)` block with this
   exact explicit logging logic:

       std::ofstream logFile("./build/api_log.txt", std::ios::app);
       if (res) {
           logFile << "[GeminiClient] HTTP Status: " << res->status << "\n";
           std::cout << "\n[GeminiClient] HTTP Status: " << res->status << std::endl;

           if (res->status == 200) {
               logFile << "[GeminiClient] Success Response:\n" << res->body << "\n\n";
               std::cout << "[GeminiClient] Success! Logged to ./build/api_log.txt" << std::endl;
               FILE* f = fopen("./build/api_response.json", "wb");
               if (f) { fwrite(res->body.c_str(), 1, res->body.size(), f); fclose(f); }
           } else {
               logFile << "[GeminiClient] API Error Body:\n" << res->body << "\n\n";
               std::cerr << "[GeminiClient] API Error logged to ./build/api_log.txt" << std::endl;
           }
       } else {
           logFile << "[GeminiClient] Network Request Failed. Error code: " << res.error() << "\n\n";
           std::cerr << "[GeminiClient] Network Failed. See api_log.txt" << std::endl;
       }
       logFile.close();

   3. SELF-HEALING RUNTIME LOOP:
      - Compile the codebase using Ninja.
      - Temporarily inject `g_State.activeTask = 3; g_State.captureRequested = true;` at the very end of your `setup()` function so the application
   fires the network payload instantly upon boot without requiring human interaction.
      - Execute `./build/bin/AliceViewer.exe` (let it run for 5 seconds, then kill the process).
      - Read `./build/api_log.txt`.
      - Iterate this build -> run -> read log sequence. Do not stop until the log explicitly confirms an HTTP 200 OK.
      - ONCE SUCCESSFUL: Remove the temporary `setup()` trigger to restore the framework to an interactive state.

 > [CLI AGENT PROMPT]
   CONTEXT:
   Initialize according to `gemini.md`. We are expanding the `AliceGeminiClient.h` pipeline in Alice Viewer 2. We are deploying a dual-task
   architecture:
   1. **Task A (Analysis):** Image-to-Text analysis of the G-Buffers.
   2. **Task B (Rendering):** Image+Text-to-Image generation, utilizing the Segmentation and Depth maps as structural stencils for photo-realistic
   output.

   CRITICAL DISCOVERIES TO INCORPORATE:
   * **The PBO Latency Trap:** The previous double-buffered PBO architecture introduced a 1-frame latency, causing the API to analyze the initial
   zero-initialized `calloc` memory (solid black images).
   * **The 404 Endpoint Shift:** `gemini-1.5-flash` currently returns an HTTP 404 in this environment. You MUST use the `gemini-flash-latest` model
   (via the `v1beta` API) which successfully resolves and returns HTTP 200 OK.

   EXECUTION MANDATE:
   Execute SOP Steps 1 through 7, adhering strictly to the newly defined 3-Phase Crucible for Step 7. **You must autonomously test and self-heal
   UNTIL meaningful results are achieved, not just 0 compiler errors.**

   1. PHASE 1 (MVP): Refactor `AliceGeminiClient.h`.
      - Strip out the double-buffered PBO (`pboIndex`, `nextPboIndex`) logic. Replace it with a strict, synchronous `glReadPixels` directly into
   the CPU heap buffers (`g_State.beautyData`, `g_State.segData`, `g_State.depthData`). Use `glPixelStorei(GL_PACK_ALIGNMENT, 1);`.
      - Implement `Task A`: POST to `gemini-flash-latest:generateContent` for text analysis.
      - Implement `Task B`: POST to the relevant Gemini Image Generation endpoint, passing the Depth/Segmentation Base64 buffers as control
   stencils/reference images along with a rendering prompt.
      - Build locally using LLVM/Ninja until 0 errors.

   2. PHASE 2 (AESTHETIC & SEMANTIC CRUCIBLE): Technical execution is insufficient; you must validate the semantic output.
      - **Pre-flight:** Verify the local disk dumps (`beauty.png`, `seg.png`, `depth.png`) immediately after the *first* capture trigger. They must
   contain actual geometry, not black silhouettes.
      - **Task A Validation:** The API response JSON must contain a meaningful spatial/visual analysis. If the AI responds with "the images are
   completely black" or similar, your readback logic is flawed. Self-heal and retry.
      - **Task B Validation:** The API must return a valid Base64 image payload. Decode it and write it to `./build/ai_render_output.png`.
      - DO NOT proceed until both tasks yield semantically valid, non-empty, meaningful results.

   3. PHASE 3 (PERFORMANCE): Ensure the synchronous `glReadPixels` does not leak memory or overflow the `AliceMemory::LinearArena`. Verify the C++
   worker thread maintains UI responsiveness during the network stall and Base64 encoding phases.

   Output your planned approach for Phase 1 and ASK FOR PERMISSION before initiating the shell build commands.

✦ Here is my planned approach for Phase 1 (MVP).

  Planned Approach for Phase 1

   1. Refactor PBO Architecture (Latency & Black Image Fix):
      - Remove Double-Buffering: Strip out pboIndex, nextPboIndex, and all glGenBuffers/glBindBuffer logic related to the async PBOs in
        AliceGeminiClient.h.
      - Synchronous Readback: In the keyPress capture block, replace the async PBO mapping with direct, synchronous glReadPixels calls straight into
        the pre-allocated CPU heap buffers (g_State.beautyData, g_State.segData, g_State.depthData).
      - Memory Alignment: Inject glPixelStorei(GL_PACK_ALIGNMENT, 1); immediately before the glReadPixels calls to guarantee tight byte packing and
        prevent row-stride corruption.

   2. Implement Task A (Analysis):
      - Endpoint: POST to /v1beta/models/gemini-flash-latest:generateContent.
      - Trigger: Configured for g_State.activeTask == 1.
      - Payload: Base64 representations of the Beauty, Segmentation, and Depth maps alongside a text prompt requesting a rigorous spatial and visual
        analysis of the scene.
      - Output: The textual response will be parsed and written to ./build/api_log.txt for semantic validation in Phase 2.

   3. Implement Task B (Rendering):
      - Endpoint: POST to /v1beta/models/gemini-flash-latest:generateContent (utilizing its 2026 native multimodal I/O capabilities) or the specific
        image generation endpoint if preferred.
      - Trigger: Configured for g_State.activeTask == 2.
      - Payload: The Depth and Segmentation Base64 buffers serving strictly as structural stencils/reference images, accompanied by a rendering
        prompt (e.g., "Render a highly detailed, photorealistic scene strictly adhering to the spatial structure and boundaries of these provided
        stencils.").
      - Output: Parse the API's JSON response for the Base64 image payload (using the existing parseGeminiResponse utility), decode it, and write
        the resulting binary data directly to ./build/ai_render_output.png.

   4. Compilation & Local Build:
      - Execute the established Windows LLVM/Ninja toolchain (clang-cl, lld-link).
      - Autonomously self-heal any C++ syntax or linkage errors until the project compiles with 0 errors.

  Please review the plan. Do I have your permission to initiate the codebase modifications and shell build commands for Phase 1?
